	OutputLine(NULL, "「…そんなに間違えないでしょ。",
		   NULL, "\"...You wouldn't have gotten that wrong.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s02/03/130300077", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "服装だって違うんだから。」",
		   NULL, " We're wearing different clothes.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//「え、......あ、......そうだよな......。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s02/01/130100205", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「え、……あ、……そうだよな……。」",
		   NULL, "\"Huh? ......Oh... ...that's right......\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　魅音のしばらくの沈黙が、じわじわと俺を締め上げる...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　魅音のしばらくの沈黙が、じわじわと俺を締め上げる…。",
		   NULL, "Mion's momentary silence was like a deathgrip upon me...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(2, 3, "portrait/me2_akuwarai_a1_", "1", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 200, TRUE );

//「......しょーがないなぁ、詩音は＠　まぁあいつのことだから、放っておいても大丈夫かな。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s02/03/130300078", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……しょーがないなぁ、詩音は！",
		   NULL, "\"...I just can't do anything about that Shion!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 3, "ps3/s02/03/130300079", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　まぁあいつのことだから、放っておいても大丈夫かな。」",
		   NULL, " Well, it's her we're talking about, so we can just leave her be.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　魅音は元の、いつもの笑顔に戻ると、俺の手を強く引き、石段を駆け下りていった...￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　魅音は元の、いつもの笑顔に戻ると、俺の手を強く引き、石段を駆け下りていった…。",
		   NULL, "Mion's expression returned to her former, usual smile, and we continued down the stone steps, her firmly pulling my hand along...", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
//■８日目幕間

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );

	Wait( 1000 );
//	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 3000 );

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/wata008", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
